<output_to_ai_assistant>
That's an excellent question regarding property surveys for a condo purchase in Toronto!

For condos, a "Full Structural Survey" (like a house survey) is generally not required for individual unit buyers, as the structural integrity of the building is the responsibility of the condo corporation, which conducts its own regular assessments.

However, for a new build condo like the one you've selected, a **New Build Inspection** is highly recommended. This specialist survey focuses on identifying any 'snags' or defects within your specific unit before you take possession. It typically costs around **CAD $400**.

Alternatively, a **Basic Survey** (CAD $300) can also be conducted to assess the general condition of the interior of your unit, identifying any essential issues.

Please note that these property surveys are **separate expenses** from the "Basic Legal Package" (CAD $800), which covers the legal aspects of contract review and conveyancing.

So, to summarize: a unit-specific inspection is recommended, and it would be an additional cost depending on the type of survey you choose.
</output_to_ai_assistant>

=== BEFORE GATEWAY FIREWALL ===

That's an excellent question regarding property surveys for a condo purchase in Toronto!

For condos, a "Full Structural Survey" (like a house survey) is generally not required for individual unit buyers, as the structural integrity of the building is the responsibility of the condo corporation, which conducts its own regular assessments.

However, for a new build condo like the one you've selected, a **New Build Inspection** is highly recommended. This specialist survey focuses on identifying any 'snags' or defects within your specific unit before you take possession. It typically costs around **CAD $400**.

Alternatively, a **Basic Survey** (CAD $300) can also be conducted to assess the general condition of the interior of your unit, identifying any essential issues.

Please note that these property surveys are **separate expenses** from the "Basic Legal Package" (CAD $800), which covers the legal aspects of contract review and conveyancing.

So, to summarize: a unit-specific inspection is recommended, and it would be an additional cost depending on the type of survey you choose.
